The text of Aristotle most relevant to this book is the [3mNicomachean Ethics [0m, available in Penguin Classics in an edition by 
Jonathan Barnes (Harmondsworth, 1976). Jonathan Barnes has also published a useful introduction to Aristotle in the Very Short 
Introduction series (Oxford, 2000), though not much of it deals with his ethical thought. See also D. S. Hutchinson, [3mThe Virtues 
of Aristotle [0m(London, 1986), and Jonathan Lear, [3mAristotle: The Desire to Understand [0m(Cambridge, 1988). 

More general studies of ethics relevant to the bookโs argument can be found in Alasdair MacIntyre, [3mA Short History of Ethics [0m
(London, 1968) and [3mAfter Virtue [0m(London, 1981). A more recent, illuminating study is Rosalind Hursthouse, [3mOn Virtue Ethics [0m
(Oxford, 1999).

Works by Nietzsche cited in this study are [3mThe Will to Power [0m(New York, 1975), [3mBeyond Good and Evil [0m, and [3mThe Birth of Tragedy [0m.

of Nietzscheโs texts. Classic introductions to his thought are Walter Kaufmann, [3mNietzsche: Philosopher, Psychologist, and

For introductions to Wittgensteinโs thought, see D. F. Pears, [3mWittgenstein [0m(London, 1971), and Anthony Kenny, [3mWittgenstein [0m

There are various allusions throughout the book to these cultural movements, which the reader might like to have further 
elucidated. For modernism, Peter Conradโs monumental [3mModern Times, Modern Places [0m(London, 1998) is worth dipping in and out of. An

Politics of Modernism [0m(London, 1989), and T. J. Clark, [3mFarewell to an Idea [0m(New Haven and London, 1999). 

For postmodernism, see Jean-Franรงois Lyotard, [3mThe Postmodern Condition [0m(Minneapolis, 1984); Ihab Hassan, [3mThe Postmodern Turn [0m
(Ithaca, NY, 1987); David Harvey, [3mThe Condition of Postmodernity [0m(Oxford, 1990); and Perry Anderson, [3mThe Origins of Postmodernity [0m
(London, 1998). Briefer studies of the trend are to be found in Alex Callinicos, [3mAgainst Postmodernism [0m, and Terry Eagleton, [3mThe 
Illusions of Postmodernism [0m(Oxford, 1996). A more difficult and substantial study is Fredric Jameson, [3mPostmodernism, or, the 
Cultural Logic of Late Capitalism [0m(Durham, NC, 1991).
